
defined_text = {
	name = Privilege_NOProcessing0Has
	text = {
		localisation_key = Privilege_NOProcessing0_G
		trigger = { Privilege_HasGreater = { Privilege=NOProcessing Lvl=0 } }
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = Privilege_NOProcessing0_R
		trigger = { NOT = { Privilege_HasGreater = { Privilege=NOProcessing Lvl=0 } } }
	}
}
